        <h2>Storyline</h2>
        
        <div class="inline canwrap" itemprop="description">
            <p>
1327: after a mysterious death in a Benedictine Abbey, the monks are convinced that the apocalypse is coming. With the Abbey to play host to a council on the Franciscan's Order's belief that the Church should rid itself of wealth, William of Baskerville, a respected Franciscan monk, is asked to assist in determining the cause of the untimely death. Alas, more deaths occur as the investigation draws closer to uncovering the secret the Abbey wants hidden, and there is finally no stopping the Holy Inquisition from taking an active hand in the process. William and his young novice must race against time to prove the innocence of the unjustly accused and avoid the wrath of Holy Inquisitor Bernardo Gui.                <em class="nobr">Written by
<a href="/search/title?plot_author=Rick Munoz <rick.munoz@his.com>&view=simple&sort=alpha"
>Rick Munoz &lt;rick.munoz@his.com&gt;</a></em>            </p>
        </div>

        <h2>Did You Know?</h2>
    <div id="trivia" class="txt-block">
        <h4>Trivia</h4>


<a href="/name/nm0889926?ref_=tt_trv_trv">Valentina Vargas</a> replaced <a href="/name/nm0000528?ref_=tt_trv_trv">Mathilda May</a> as The Girl. May had to turn down the role because she was in a tight schedule with <a href="/title/tt0089489?ref_=tt_trv_trv">Lifeforce - Die t&ouml;dliche Bedrohung</a> (1985).        <a href="trivia?ref_=tt_trv_trv"
class="nobr" >See more</a>  &raquo;
    </div>
                <hr />
     <div id="goofs"  class="txt-block">
        <h4>Goofs</h4>
The near-full plate armor worn by the guards for the Inquisition is at least a century too early.        <a href="trivia?tab=gf&ref_=tt_trv_gf"
class="nobr" >See more</a>  &raquo;
    </div>   
                <hr />
    <div id="quotes" class="text-block">
        <h4>Quotes</h4>
[<span class="fine">first lines</span>]
<br /><a href="/name/nm0919327/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"
><span class="character">Voice of Adso as an Old Man</span></a>:
Having reached the end of my poor sinner's life, my hair now white, I prepare to leave on this parchment my testimony as to the wondrous and terrible events that I witnessed in my youth, towards the end of the year of our Lord 1327. May God grant me the wisdom and grace to be the faithful chronicler of the happenings that took place in a remote abbey in the dark north of Italy. An abbey whose name it seems, even now, pious and prudent to omit.
<br />        <a href="trivia?tab=qt&ref_=tt_trv_qu"
class="nobr" >See more</a> &raquo;
    </div>

    <div class="article" id="titleUserReviewsTeaser">
        <h2>User Reviews</h2>
        <div class="user-comments">
                    <div class="tinystarbar" title="10/10">
                        <div style="width: 100px;">&nbsp;</div>
                    </div>
                <span itemprop="review" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">  
                    <strong itemprop="name">Unforgettable.... after all these years</strong>
                    <span itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                        <meta itemprop="worstRating" content = "1" />
                        <meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="10" />
                        <meta itemprop="bestRating" content="10" />
                    </span>
                    <div class="comment-meta">
                        3 September 2006 | by <a href="/user/ur11987804/?ref_=tt_urv"
><span itemprop="author">lims_home</span></a>
                        <meta itemprop="datePublished" content="2006-09-03" />
                              (Singapore)
                        &ndash; <a href="/user/ur11987804/comments?ref_=tt_urv"
>See all my reviews</a>
                    </div>
                    <div>
                        <p itemprop="reviewBody">I first saw this film 20 years ago. This was in the cinema when it first came out. I was too young at that time to fully comprehend some of the subtleties of the movie. Whilst I enjoyed the whodunit aspects, I was disturbed by some of the images that were presented. The self-flagellation by Savaltore is an image which stays in mind till today. Since then, I&#39;ve watched it every 2 years or so, and the amazing thing is that each time I get more and more out of the film. Sometimes, it&#39;s the greater awareness of the religious issues of those times; sometimes it&#39;s because the actors have since become more recognised (eg Christian Slater, Ron Perlman (Hellboy!)). The cinematography is excellent, acting superb. An unforgettable film and highly recommended.</p>
                    </div>
                </span>
                <hr />
                <div class="yn" id="ynd_1465411">
